Spoiler File -- Monsters (PosChengband 4.0.0)        Home

The Filthy street urchin  (L.Dark 't')
=== Num:1  Lev:0  Rar:2  Spd:+0  Hp:1d4  Ac:1  Exp:0
He looks squalid and thoroughly revolting.
He lives in the town, and moves a bit erratically at normal speed. A kill
of this evil human thief is worth about 0.00 points for a 1st level
character. He usually appears in groups. He has an armor rating of 1 and a
life rating of 1d4. He can open doors and pick up objects. He will evolve
into Agent of black market when he gets enough experience. He takes quite
a while to see intruders, which he may notice from 40 feet. He can beg, and
touch to steal gold.

=== Num:2  Lev:0  Rar:3  Spd:+0  Hp:1d2  Ac:1  Exp:0

It lives in the town, and moves a bit erratically at normal speed. A kill
of this natural creature is worth about 0.00 points for a 1st level
character. It has an armor rating of 1 and a life rating of 1d2. It will
evolve into Wild cat when it gets enough experience. It is fairly observant
of intruders, which it may notice from 300 feet. It can claw to attack with
damage 1d3.

[U] Farmer Maggot  (White 'h')
=== Num:8  Lev:0  Rar:3  Spd:+0  Hp:350  Ac:10  Exp:0
Before you appears a broad thick-set hobbit with a round red face. "What's
wrong with old Maggot?" asked Pippin. "He's a good friend to all the
Brandybucks. Of course he's a terror to trespassers, and keeps ferocious
dogs -- but after all, folk down here are near the border and have to be
more on their guard." 
He lives in the town, and moves at normal speed. Killing this creature is
worth about 0.00 points for a 1st level character. He has an armor rating
of 10 and a life rating of 350. He can illuminate the dungeon, open doors
and bash down doors. He cannot be confused or slept. He is very observant
of intruders, which he may notice from 400 feet. He may carry an
exceptional object. He can moan, moan, and hit to attack with damage 1d5.

The Blinking dot  (Slate ',')
=== Num:22  Lev:1  Rar:1  Spd:+0  Hp:1d2  Ac:1  Exp:3
Is it there or is it not? 
It is normally found on dungeon level 1, won't be found deeper than dungeon
level 10, and moves at normal speed, but does not deign to chase intruders.
A kill of this creature is worth about 1.00 point for a 1st level
character. It is magical, casting spells which blink-self; 50% of the time.
It has an armor rating of 1 and a life rating of 1d2. It is not detected by
telepathy. It resists poison. It won't evolve. It cannot be frightened,
confused or slept. It is ever vigilant for intruders, which it may notice
from 20 feet. It can release spores to confuse with damage 1d6.

[U] Greater Hell-Beast  (Slate 'U')
=== Num:39  Lev:1  Rar:6  Spd:+5  Hp:1500  Ac:100  Exp:250
This unholy abomination will crush you. Flee while you can!
It is normally found on dungeon level 1, and moves somewhat quickly.
Killing this evil demon is worth about 83.33 points for a 1st level
character. It is magical, casting spells which blink-self, teleport-self or
teleport away; 11% of the time. It has an armor rating of 100 and a life
rating of 1500. It can bore through walls. It resists acid, lightning,
fire, cold, poison, light, dark, nether, water, plasma, shards, sound,
chaos, nexus, disenchantment, force, inertia, time and gravity. It pays
very little attention to intruders, which it may notice from 100 feet. It
can gaze to attack, gaze to attack, and crush to attack.

=== Num:63  Lev:3  Rar:2  Spd:+20  Hp:400  Ac:12  Exp:18
"Down the face of a precipice, sheer and almost smooth it seemed in the
pale moonlight, a small black shape was moving with its thin limbs splayed
out. Maybe its soft clinging hands and toes were used, but it looked as if
it was just creeping down on sticky pads, like some large prowling thing of

of a dungeon.
